Current Commentary

Observations on the Great Coup in Japan 19

— Ji

The turbulent Japanese political situation has now undergone a dramatic change. The news has shocked us. The severity of this coup is beyond comparison with the May 15th Incident. It is difficult to predict how it will develop in the future, but by examining the past Japanese political situation, we can learn some of the meanings of this coup. Please allow me to explain them separately:

First, since the September 18th Incident, young Japanese soldiers have gained power due to the gradual victories in foreign aggression. They even want to seize all political power. Therefore, they first created the May 15th Incident, and now they have expanded it and caused this huge change. The May 15th Incident was a fierce attack by young military groups on parliamentary politics, while this incident is a decisive battle between radical elements in political parties and right-wing military groups against elders, senior ministers, and stable elements in political parties. In other words, it is a decisive key moment in the rise and fall of fascist forces and the power of feudal nobles and industrial capitalists.

Second, although the brewing of this incident was not a day's work, the most recent reasons for promoting this coup, according to our observation, are several: The result of the recent general election was that the Minseitō won a great victory, and the position of the Okada Cabinet turned stable, which was the opposite of the desire of young Japanese soldiers to have the Okada Cabinet resign immediately. Moreover, there was a special phenomenon in this general election, that is, the old bureaucratic and aristocratic forces strengthened their alliance and suppressed young soldiers under the slogan of "national unity and cooperation." The murder of Nagata Tetsuzan in July last year was a serious warning from Japanese reservists to the stable faction of the military. This matter has not yet been resolved, and the situation has become more complicated. When General Masaki Jinzaburō, the leader of the young military faction, appeared in court on the 25th of this month as a witness in the Nagata incident public trial, he refused to answer the judge's questions because they involved official secrets and angrily withdrew from the court. However, the defense side insisted on Masaki clarifying the truth, and the government also intended to investigate the matter. Recently, Russian-Japanese relations have been tense. The opinions of the young faction of the Japanese military were in obvious opposition with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and senior ministers. The young faction of the military intended to fight Russia without hesitation, while the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and senior ministers believed that Russian-Japanese relations must be eased. The young faction of the military believed that the Okada Cabinet was weak and incompetent and must be overthrown. Dr. Minobe Tatsukichi, whose theory of the Emperor as an organ of the state became the target of attacks by various factions of the military, was assassinated on the 21st of this month but was not killed. The arrested perpetrator admitted that he was related to right-wing violent military groups. With these four reasons, yesterday's huge coup was facilitated.

Moreover, the targeting of Finance Minister Takahashi and Prime Minister Okada as the main targets of the assassination has its important reasons. We all know that the military is strongly advocating the healthy naval and army theory, advocating expanding armaments as much as possible, while Finance Minister Takahashi is a powerful figure in opposing the unlimited expansion of the military budget and has won the support of the Japanese business and financial circles. Although Prime Minister Okada came from the military, his policies were consistent with the senior ministers. Since taking office, he has made considerable efforts to suppress right-wing military groups. As of the end of August last year, the number of people arrested in violent groups has reached more than 20,000. (According to China United News Agency) The resentment of right-wing military groups has been around for a long time.

The causes of this coup are extremely complex, and its impact on Japanese politics will inevitably be significant. The future evolution will have a significant reflection on the entire China-Japan relationship. This is what we must pay attention to.

Florentine's Speech: Supporting the Franco-Russian Agreement, Collective Security Maintains Peace, Not a Military Alliance, Welcoming Germany to Participate in Cooperation 20

Paris - French Foreign Minister Florentine delivered a brilliant speech in the Chamber of Deputies today, supporting the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement, stating that this agreement is not a military alliance, but only a confirmation of the Locarno Pact and a stage on the road to peace. After Florentine's speech, the entire left wing and most of the central party cheered enthusiastically. When the new agreement is voted on by the Chamber of Deputies tomorrow, it will undoubtedly be passed. However, the Foreign Minister failed to sway the opposition of the right wing parties, who were reluctant to have any close alliance with Moscow. They belittled the Soviet Union's military strength and did not want to provoke Germany unnecessarily. However, the Foreign Minister stated that he intended to submit the question of whether the agreement complied with the Locarno Pact to the Hague Court for a ruling, and therefore won a victory.

At the beginning of his speech, Florentine stated that once the agreement was passed, it would consolidate the organization of European collective security. France has never given up its willingness to invite Germany to participate in understandings aimed at safeguarding peace. All previous governments have been faithful to this concept, and have always been careful to keep Germany's access open. The agreement does not contain obligations that can be found in alliance treaties, and does not violate the spirit of the Locarno Pact. The agreement confirms the Locarno Pact and declares that it must not be aggressive towards Germany. The agreement only seeks to resist aggressors. Florentine then quoted government statements, declaring and referring to cooperation with the Germans. His conclusion was: "A great country that owes so much to culture should be restored to an equal position in the world. This is what we desire." (Reuters, 26th)

Paris - This afternoon at 3:00 PM, the Chamber of Deputies convened, continuing the debate on the ratification of the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty. Foreign Minister Florentine, after several days of Chamber meetings, addressed the various criticisms of the treaty. At today's meeting, he personally delivered a speech to provide a general response. The speech was very long, lasting two hours. The gist of his remarks was, "Signing the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty is our inherent right. If Germany formally challenges our recognition of this right, we will submit this issue to the Hague International Permanent Court for a ruling." He then outlined that since 1920, the French government's entire policy has been to advance towards the goal of maintaining peace through the path of collective security. Collective security is the objective pursued by the League of Nations. Although there have been changes in successive governments, this policy has remained consistent. As for the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty, all countries except Germany view it with a sympathetic attitude, because this treaty does not go beyond the framework of the League of Nations, and it is open for all countries to join. Moreover, the two signatory countries of the treaty have agreed to abide by any proposals put forward by the League of Nations. Therefore, it cannot be compared with the offensive and defensive alliances before the European War. If critics argue that if something happens in Eastern Europe, France will be bound by this treaty and drawn into the vortex, the answer is that at the beginning of the Great War in 1914, the motive for the outbreak had nothing to do with us (referring to the assassination of the Austrian Crown Prince). If countries such as Britain and Italy had adopted a selfish and isolationist stance, they could have stood idly by and not joined our side. Therefore, concluding a mutual assistance treaty and being drawn into a war vortex should not be confused."

Florentine's conclusion was very moving, asking the deputies not to mix domestic political issues with foreign policy. For example, the Italian political system and the Soviet political system are diametrically opposed, but the friendly relations between Italy and Russia are very clear. (Havas, 25th)

According to those familiar with the political situation, observing the situation in the Chamber of Deputies, when the Chamber votes on this bill, although the number of votes in favor may not be as many as those who have consistently supported the government's foreign policy, it will undoubtedly be a majority. Generally speaking, the Chamber of Deputies will vote to pass the ratification on Thursday, and then send it to the Senate. Repeated debates in the Senate will also take a considerable amount of time. Therefore, the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty may not be ratified by both houses of parliament before March 3. By then, the Chamber of Deputies' re-election is approaching, and the current session will soon end. If it is delayed in this way, the stance of France and other countries on this treaty may change. (Havas News Agency, 26th)

Germany's Attitude Towards the Franco-Russian Agreement: Believes it is Incompatible with the Locarno Pact, No Severe Steps Will Be Taken at Present 21

Berlin - Informed sources here believe that Germany will not formally challenge the Locarno Pact at present. The approval of the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement is sufficient to destroy Germany's trust in the Locarno Pact, but Germany does not need to take severe steps to challenge the agreement now. Political circles here firmly declare that Germany considers the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement and the Locarno Pact to be incompatible. (Reuters, 26th)

Italy and Germany Seek Closer Ties: Europe Draws a New Divide, Five Countries Organize a Group, Dealing with the Common Front of Britain and France 22

London - Today, newspapers here are filled with reports that as a result of the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement and the Anglo-French sanctions policy against Italy, European powers may draw a new divide. Newspapers also carry rumors from Rome that after Mussolini's meeting with the German Ambassador to Italy, Hassel, a compromise has been reached. If the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement is passed by the French Chamber of Deputies, Italy and Germany will take joint action. The general impression is that a group of five countries, Germany, Italy, Austria, Hungary, and Poland, is currently being formed in Rome. Italian authorities and diplomatic circles in Rome acknowledge that extremely important secret negotiations are currently underway. It is said that after Hassel's meeting with Mussolini, the Polish Ambassador to Rome immediately visited Mussolini and suddenly returned to his country. Suvich, the Austrian Foreign Minister, who unexpectedly met with him in Florence last week, is now planning to reciprocate with a visit to the Hungarian capital. Therefore, Italian diplomacy, which had not focused on European affairs since the start of the Italian-Abyssinian War, is now fully active again. It is widely believed that Mussolini is now trying to make all countries feel that if the Stresa Front collapses, there will be dire consequences. (Reuters, 26th)

Rome - Political circles here dismiss with a smile the rumors that Italy and Germany have reached an agreement challenging the Locarno Pact. However, newspapers are still filled with threatening remarks, saying that if sanctions against Italy continue, Italy will eventually challenge the Pact. They also claim that the possibility of Poland joining the Italy-Germany group is currently being discussed. (Reuters, 25th)

Warsaw - Since Prussian Premier and German Aviation Minister General Goering recently visited here, the issue of Poland joining an agreement with Germany has attracted much attention. However, due to disagreements between the two countries, although the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement has been severely criticized by Poland, Poland does not seem likely to accept Germany as its new comrade. (Reuters, 25th)

Important Anglo-Belgian Talks 23

London - According to our correspondent, important talks are currently being held here between Britain and Belgium. The Belgian representative is Count de Lantsheere (who attended the funeral of the late King George V), and the British representative is Mr. Sargent of the Foreign Office (who was a member of the British delegation to the Paris Peace Conference in 1919). The following issues are considered important: If the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty is ratified by the French Parliament, Germany may demand revisions to the regulations regarding the demilitarized zone of the Rhineland and the Locarno Pact. What stance should Britain and Belgium take at that time? According to Belgian sources here, the Flemish people of Belgium are now vigorously advocating that Belgium should revert to a neutral system, guaranteed by Britain, Germany, and France, just as it was before the European War. (Note: Belgium has two ethnic groups, one is the Walloon people, who belong to the Latin system and whose language and customs are similar to those of France, and the other is the Flemish people, who belong to the Teutonic system and are close to the Dutch people). (Havas, 26th)

Afghan Foreign Minister Visits Berlin 24

Berlin - Afghan Foreign Minister Muhammid arrived here today and plans to stay for several days. (National Telegram, 25th)

Britain Plans to Conclude a Tripartite Naval Treaty with the United States and Germany, in Order to Threaten France and Italy into Submission, but France Insists on Concluding a Quadripartite Agreement, Negotiations in London are Still in Complicated Discussions

London - The Associated Press learned from reliable sources today that Britain has informally suggested that if the London Naval Conference fails, Britain, the United States, and Germany should conclude a naval agreement. It is said that this proposal is the result of Britain's dissatisfaction with the European political issues raised by the French and Italian representatives. Today, the U.S. representatives refused to discuss their feelings about this proposal. If Britain, the United States, and Germany form an agreement, they should exchange documents and reserve space for future conferences, and Japan and Russia may be invited to participate. (National Telegram, 25th)

London - France is extremely opposed to Britain's proposed tripartite naval treaty between Britain, the United States, and Germany, which would leave France and Italy out of the picture. Therefore, it has put forward another proposal today: The current London Naval Conference can only conclude a quadripartite agreement, limited to Britain, the United States, France, and Italy. Only in this way can France join in signing, and Italy can follow suit. (National Telegram, 25th)

London - The London Naval Conference today discussed the renewal of the naval treaty between Britain and Germany, in order to prevent the naval conference from reaching a deadlock due to European political issues. France opposes inviting Germany to sign the treaty. In order to accommodate France's wishes, there is now a positive proposal to suggest that Britain and Germany conduct separate negotiations on qualitative aspects of the treaty to supplement the existing quantitative aspects of the treaty between Britain and Germany. It is reported that Mr. Craig of the British Foreign Office has discussed this with the naval attaché of the German Embassy today. This solution can reconcile the opinions of Britain, the United States, and France. If Italy can also comply, the naval treaty can be signed and submitted to Japan. However, Italy has stated that it is unwilling to sign the treaty while sanctions are in effect. This attitude has not changed, so it is expected that the discussions on the oil embargo in Geneva next week will be closely related to Italy's attitude at the London Naval Conference. (Reuters, 25th)

Berlin - Official circles today implicitly indicated that if the tripartite naval treaty does not hinder the interests of Germany in the Anglo-German naval agreement, Germany will welcome the tripartite naval treaty. There are three reasons why Germany welcomes this tripartite agreement: 1. The establishment of this agreement can recognize Germany's claim to be a first-class naval power. 2. It can show the consistency of Germany with other Anglo-Saxon nations. 3. It can show the different trends of Britain, the United States, and France. (National Telegram, 25th)

London - Those close to the naval conference negotiations are now worried that the return of Italian chief delegate Piaccia to London may bring the naval conference to a standstill, and the qualitative restriction plan that has actually been agreed upon will be hindered. Most of the qualitative compromises are based on the standards of existing treaties, with the only exceptions being the stipulation that cruisers will be 8,000 tons instead of 10,000 tons, and aircraft carriers will be 23,000 tons instead of 27,000 tons. The largest financial savings are only in the cruiser area, with an estimated savings of 300,000 pounds per vessel. However, the savings originally hoped for by Britain were even greater than this, and focused especially on battleships. Britain's battleship limit was 25,000 tons, but the current agreement is for battleships of 35,000 tons, a difference of 3 million pounds. The scope of Britain's rearmament program and its extent can only be announced by officials next week, but private estimates put the cost at 300 million pounds, with the navy accounting for the largest share. It is heard that Britain will use the entire empire as a unit to manage armaments, so the establishment of a naval agreement is very important. Only with this can there be a solid foundation for official estimates. The methods proposed by France and Italy are not welcome. The future naval treaty will be accompanied by a protocol, explaining the desire and method of seeking the signatures of Japan, Germany, and Russia in the future. The current difficulty lies in the drafting of this protocol. France believes that allowing Germany to participate in the naval conference is tantamount to recognizing the existence of a German navy that deviates from the law, and forgiving Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles, so it has always been unwilling for Germany to join. There are now rumors that Germany intends to reoccupy the demilitarized Rhineland area to counter the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Agreement. France's attitude of rejecting Germany's participation in the naval conference will not change because of this. France is now willing to sign any naval treaty first, but requires the insertion of a clause in the protocol, the main purpose of which is to make France's final signature conditional on the establishment of a general European arms agreement. Italy has the same view, and also requires a method regarding sanctions, which has aroused opposition from the US representatives. The US representatives have stated to British Foreign Secretary Eden that they came here to sign a naval treaty, and the US position does not allow it to participate in European disputes. Looking at the above situation, people here are mostly worried that the naval conference discussions are nearing a deadlock, and the results already obtained may be lost. Last night, British Foreign Secretary Eden repeatedly stated in the House of Commons that Britain would soon be engaged in a large-scale rearmament. This statement has aroused speculation about who will be the head of the new national defense agency in charge of the army, navy, and air force. Some people expect former Foreign Secretary Hoare to be the head, but today's newspapers say that Finance Minister Neville Chamberlain is the most promising. (Reuters, 25th)

London - Informed sources predict that the development of the naval conference will reach the following two results: 1. Britain, France, Italy, and the United States will sign a qualitative naval agreement. 2. Britain and Germany will separately establish a special agreement, with each country agreeing to fulfill the provisions of the four-nation agreement. However, some people fear that Germany may take the opportunity to demand a reward, and may request revisions to the provisions of the Locarno Pact and the demilitarized zone along the Rhine. If so, the negotiations will inevitably be delayed. Today, someone spread rumors that if the naval conference fails, Britain will sign a treaty with the United States alone, or even with Germany. This statement was denied by responsible naval officials, who said that this news was due to a misunderstanding of the recent developments in the naval conference. As far as is generally known, Britain is currently conducting negotiations with Germany, and its purpose is to get Germany to sign and join the four-nation agreement. If Germany agrees, it is sufficient to add a clause to the Anglo-German naval agreement (signed last June) to clarify it, so that France can avoid signing a naval agreement with Germany, and the naval provisions of the Treaty of Versailles will not be violated. This is the best of both worlds. Regarding the negotiations between Britain and Germany, it is now known that the first decision was made last night at the German Embassy in Britain, and the second decision was made at 4:00 PM today at the Foreign Office. The British representative is Craig, a specialist at the Foreign Office, and the German representative is Wiesner, the naval attaché of the embassy. According to reports in the German capital, Germany has not opposed this negotiation process. Based on the above circumstances and the information obtained by our correspondent this morning, it can be summarized into two points: 1. A qualitative naval limitation agreement can be signed by Britain, France, Italy, and the United States this week. 2. Britain originally planned to seek Germany's consent before signing the four-nation agreement, but has now abandoned this plan. The above two pieces of information can be said to have been confirmed. (Havas, 25th)

Naval Mutual Assistance Issue: Italy Sends Note to Britain and France, Reserving the Right to Re-Discuss 25

Paris - Regarding the issue of naval mutual assistance among countries along the Mediterranean coast, Italy had previously protested to Britain, and Britain replied on January 23. This morning, Italian Ambassador to Britain Grandi submitted a note from the Italian government to the British Foreign Office. Currently, Italian Ambassador to France Cerutti also delivered a note from the Italian government on this issue to Foreign Minister Florentine, the content of which is exactly the same as the one submitted by Grandi to the British Foreign Office this morning. It states that the Italian government still maintains its original position on this issue, and says, "The Italian government still reserves the right to re-discuss this issue at an appropriate time." (Havas, 25th)

International Commercial Telegram 39

Special Commercial News Telegram from Reuters, February 26

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price - Today is 141 shillings and a halfpence, up two and a half pence.

London Bar Silver: The silver market is stable. The spot price is 19 and three-quarter pence, and the futures price is 19 and six-eighths pence. Both are unchanged. India is buying, and China is selling.

New York Silver Market: The futures market was quiet today. The opening price for the March contract was unchanged, still at 44.64-44.90.

Exchange Rates:

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market, the price of the pound sterling opened this morning, denominated in US dollars, was slightly weaker. The Anglo-American exchange rate was 4 yuan 9 jiao 9 fen 0625 at 10:30 AM, 4375 lower than the American closing price yesterday. It continued to fall 125 half an hour later, and was 4 yuan 9 jiao 8 fen 9375. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, all the losses in the morning were recovered and it was still 4 yuan 9 jiao 9 fen 0625.

Securities:

The New York Stock Market continued to decline in trading this morning, with various securities falling across the board, especially steel, hardware, railways, and automobiles. Later, due to strong buying, market prices rebounded, such as public stocks. Department stores and automobile stocks are all like this. The market trend is mixed, but the sentiment is still good. The New York stock market prices are listed on the left.

Cotton and Wheat:

New York Cotton Market: The market opened steadily today, with prices higher than yesterday's closing price. Merchants believe that the news from Washington has constructive qualities, so they tend to be bullish. Prices are four to six pounds higher than yesterday. The market situation was slightly looser later, but the general trend is upward.

Liverpool Cotton: The futures market fell slightly today. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the May contract fell three pounds and was 5.65.

Chicago Wheat: The market is quiet, lacking stimulating factors. The coarse grains market is stable, due to the lack of continuity and the existence of replenishments.

Liverpool Wheat: The market opened quietly. The March contract was lower than expected due to bullish liquidations. Later, it was heard that some Australian wheat was sold, and prices rose slightly as a result, but this statement has not yet been confirmed. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the March contract price was 6 shillings and one and a half pence. The market situation is weak and has not been affected by the news of the Japanese military coup.

Rubber:

London: The rubber market fell due to news about the Akron strike being unfavorable to the market. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, the transaction price for the April-June contract was 7 pence 3125, 0625 lower than yesterday's closing price.

New York: The rubber market was weak due to disappointing news about the strike. The Rubber Restriction Committee's failure to issue a communiqué was also a reason for merchants to hesitate. But the general sentiment in the market is still stable. The New York commodity market prices are listed on the left.

Hebei-Chahar Political Council, Foreign Affairs Committee Held Meeting Yesterday 41

Beiping: The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council held its first plenary meeting this morning. Chen Zhongfu, Xiong Shaohao, Zhou Longguang, and others attended. They reported on the various diplomatic contacts made since the establishment of the Foreign Affairs Committee. The meeting adjourned for lunch at 12:00. (26th, Special Dispatch)

Beiping: The Foreign Affairs Committee of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council held its second plenary meeting at 10:00 AM on the 26th. Chairman Chen Zhongfu reported on the general situation of work. A Japanese ship, the Minko Maru, was transporting smuggled salt and was seized by the Changlu Customs Inspection Office. After negotiations with the Japanese side, they agreed to stop the smuggling. Japanese vagrants were using counterfeit currency. After negotiations, strict measures were taken to suppress it. A case involving Korean Kang Yujun and others, holding residence permits from the Tianjin Japanese Military Police, seeking housing in Potou Town, Jiahe County, was negotiated. They have agreed not to issue similar documents in the future, but hope that the council will provide appropriate convenience for legitimate Japanese businessmen traveling back and forth in the future. The meeting passed the committee's document processing procedures. It is heard that there was a detailed discussion on Hebei-Chahar foreign affairs. The meeting adjourned at 12:00. (26th, Central News Agency)

Japanese Garrison in North China to be Expanded in May 42

With Kōzuki, Tada, and Doihara as Heads

Tokyo: The Army authorities intend to expand the forces stationed in China after the adjournment of the special Diet session in May. Therefore, in the personnel reshuffle in March, Lieutenant General Kōzuki, commander of the 12th Division, and Colonel Kita, chief of the China Section of the General Staff Headquarters, were appointed to important positions with the General Staff Headquarters with a transfer of opportunity. Kōzuki will be the commander of the forces stationed in China, and Kita will be his chief of staff. Also, Major General Doihara, head of the Fengtian Special Agency of the Kwantung Army Headquarters, was transferred to the headquarters of the forces stationed in China, stationed in North China, and cooperated with Kōzuki, Kita, and others. He will be tasked with contacting the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee. Colonel Nagami, the current chief of staff of the forces stationed in China, will succeed Colonel Kita as chief of the China Section of the General Staff Headquarters. (26th, Domei News Agency)

Rural Life Talks 54

— Shao Shiping

Land Relations and Taxes in Sichuan

In people's minds, Sichuan always seems to be a chaotic world or a mysterious place, and few people have paid attention to it. Since the "Red Bandits" sneaked in, followed by the army's suppression, the voices of developing Sichuan have also risen, coupled with Mr. Ding Wenjiang's high opinion of "retreating to China's Kamchatka (referring to Sichuan, Guizhou)" Then Sichuan was noticed by everyone.

Sichuan is the largest region in the inland eighteen provinces, and various modes of production still exist: such as Songpan, the Russian side of Luo Bian and other places, still living a nomadic life. In the southwestern border of Sichuan, many places still have the remains of ethnic economies. And Chongqing has fully demonstrated the sprout of capitalism. But for the most part, it stays in the semi-feudal rural economy. What is described in this article is only this part

According to the statistics of the National Government's Accounting Office, the total area of ​​farmland in the province is 96,272,000 mu, the soil is fertile, and rice, soybeans, vegetables, fruits, tobacco, tea, hemp, cotton, etc. have great outputs. The area of ​​japonica rice in the province is 41,515,000 mu, which can produce 132,451,530 zu (100 jin). The area of ​​glutinous rice is 4,332,000 mu, which can produce 12,924,290 dan of rice. Soybeans can produce about 9 million dan, and cotton 600,000 dan. The production volume of other items is also very large. Therefore, calling it "Tianfu" is indeed "consistent with its name." However, since the Republic of China, more than 400,000 soldiers have been raised in Sichuan, and warlords have fought each other in more than 470 large and small battles. In this process, the semi-feudal relations of production have played a powerful role, and exorbitant taxes, high rents, and heavy exploitation have become increasingly rampant. Disasters of waterlogging, drought, soldiers and bandits have further accelerated the collapse of the rural economy. The peasants, under this multiple oppression, had no choice but to lose their land, flee, and starve. On the other hand, land rights are concentrated, thus brewing a serious problem.

1. The Process of Land Concentration

It is interesting to observe the extent to which land rights have been concentrated in Sichuan. However, on the one hand, there is no appropriate statistical data at present. On the other hand, "Sichuan soldiers are all big landlords." This is what we are used to hearing. For example, Yang Sen, Deng Xihou, etc., none of them are not "land connected by thousands of acres, fields separated by several counties." Their property is "rich enough to rival a country." Don't Liu Xiang and others have their own banks? Naturally, their land cannot be investigated. Generally speaking, landlords occupy more than 70% of Sichuan's land, which will not be too far from the truth. For example, in a relatively affluent Changshou County, the number of landlords and rich peasants only accounts for 15% of the total, and the land occupied accounts for 78%: the number of poor peasants is 65.9%, and the land occupied accounts for only about 8%.

Landlords and rich peasants, especially in Sichuan, are inconvenient to separate. Because they are often one and the same. And Sichuan also does not have large-scale tenant farming by rich peasants, so we calculate them together. Here we can clearly see that the landlords and rich peasants, who account for the least number of farming households (15.7%), occupy nearly eight-tenths of the land. The poor peasants, who have the largest number of entries (65.9%), own less than one-tenth of the land. The depth of land concentration can be imagined.

The statistics of 2,763 village households surveyed in Ba County in the 23rd year, although not very accurate, can also tell us the same result. According to these statistics, there are 171 landlords with more than 100 mu of land (less than 7%). Among them, there are 3 large landlords with more than 1,000 mu, 66 with more than 500 mu, and 57 with more than 200 mu. There are 94 households with more than 50 mu of land, 348 with more than 20 mu, and 350 with more than 10 mu. There are 1,500 households with less than 10 mu, accounting for nearly six-tenths of the total village households. Among them, the most pitiful poor peasants with less than 5 mu are 1,110 households. Under the current production situation in Sichuan, ordinary village households with 20 mu of land are only enough to support a family of eight. And now in Ba County near Chongqing, those with less than 10 mu account for six-tenths, naturally they are all poor peasants who cannot support themselves.

However, the terrible situation does not stop there. As a result of years of internal chaos and exorbitant taxes and levies, the degree of poverty among peasants is deepening day by day. At first, they sold grain and pawned clothes and furniture to cope. Finally, they had to pawn or sell their only means of production—land—to fill the insatiable desires of warlords and landlords. Therefore, as they are running on the road to landlessness day by day, land rights are continuing to concentrate faster. We only need to see the number of self-cultivating farmers decreasing year by year, and the number of tenant farmers increasing year by year, and this fact can be fully exposed.

Table of the increase and decrease of tenant farmers and self-cultivating farmers in Sichuan (see Agricultural Information Report of the Central Agricultural Experimental Institute)

Year % of Tenant Farmers % of Self-Cultivating Farmers % of Semi-Self-Cultivating Farmers

Republic of China Year 1 51 30 19

Republic of China Year 20 56 25 19

Republic of China Year 21 58 23 19

Republic of China Year 22 59 22 19

It can be seen that except for the semi-self-cultivating farmers who have not changed, the proportion of tenant farmers is increasing year by year, while the number of self-cultivating farmers is decreasing year by year. According to another statistic (see Oriental Magazine, Volume 24, Issue 16), tenant farmers in northern Sichuan accounted for only 28% of the total number of farmers in the first year of the Republic of China. By the 13th year of the Republic of China, it increased to 35%. Let's say it's 50% now! (According to the statistics of the Central Agricultural Experimental Institute, it is 59%) Then its rate of increase is really amazing. But in any case, this is precisely proving that the degree of polarization is developing. At the same time, we also need to point out that the reason why semi-self-cultivating farmers have not changed is not because their situation is particularly good. In fact, they are also on the road to landlessness, but only because the decline of self-cultivating farmers makes their proportion not much change!

2. Tenant Relations

As mentioned above, landlords occupy at least 70% of Sichuan's farmland, and the proportion of tenant farmers is around 60%. However, these many tenant farmers can never be compared with agricultural capitalists who operate on a large scale in Europe and the United States. Undoubtedly, they are making a living on zero-scale land. Perpetual tenancy and contract tenancy coexist. The high rent forces the tenant farmers' lives to deteriorate day by day. Now let's look at the situation in Ba County.

Rent Rate and Amount of Rent Paid by Tenant Farmers in Ba County (Surveyed in the 23rd Year)

Normal Yield Annual Yield Annual Money Rent Official Rent Additional Products Tax Payment Additional Products Deposit

Superior Land 18 Dou 10 Dou 17 Yuan 70% 2 Yuan 10 Yuan

Medium Land 15 Dou 8.5 Dou 10 Yuan 60% 1.5 Yuan 8 Yuan

Inferior Land 14 Dou 8 Dou 5 Yuan 50% 8 Jiao 6 Yuan

Ba County is close to the metropolis of Chongqing City, but the high rents in the countryside are simply unbelievable. The lowest is 50%, and the highest is more than 70%. The tenant farmers' products are not only completely occupied by the landlords in the surplus value part, but even the wage part is also deprived. Who can still recognize this as capitalist rent?

Let's cite Rong County to see its tenancy situation.

1. Money Rent - Dry land is 3 yuan per mu per year, and fenced gardens are 4 yuan.

2. Produce Rent - Paddy fields are 1 Shi per mu per year, and dry land is 2 Dou.

3. The percentage of the harvest amount - Paddy fields are 70%, gardens are 50%, and dry land is 30%.

4. Extra demand - There are local products such as chickens, ducks, vegetables, and fruits as gifts.

5. Rent reduction measures in famine years - The tenants prepare a banquet and invite the landlord to inspect. At the time of rent collection, the landlord unilaterally decides, dividing 60% for the landlord and 40% for the tenant, or 70% for the landlord and 30% for the tenant.

Oh my god! The rent is so high, but it doesn't count, and you have to receive a huge amount of interest-free deposit; it doesn't count, and you have to give extra gifts; it doesn't count, and you have to invite the landlord to eat wine in famine years; it doesn't count, and you have to do several days of unpaid labor for the landlord in many places; it doesn't count, and you have to pay taxes for the landlord! (For example, in Jianyang, although the landowners pay the regular grain for the land tax, the various additional taxes are divided 60% for the landlord and 40% for the tenant, or half for the landlord and tenant, or even completely borne by the tenant farmer. However, this is not very bad. In many places, even the regular grain is paid by the tenant farmer.)

In addition, there is a way of exploitation that cannot be named, so it is called "hard knocking." Extract a section of the Sichuan Provincial Government's circular to clarify the truth: "...In the ninth year of the Republic of China, Cheng Rentian Flower Rui Temple Property (later returned to the Education Bureau - author) An Rentian (deposit - author) was 3,200 strings. At that time, the value of silver yuan was 2,100 to 2,200 Wen per yuan. According to the current price, it should be converted into more than 1,450 silver yuan. In the 19th year, an additional deposit of 2,800 strings was added. At that time, each yuan was worth 15 strings, which should be converted into 186 yuan. This year (the 21st year), when the tenancy was withdrawn, the Education Bureau only refunded 400 yuan in foreign currency, resulting in a loss of more than 1,200 yuan." This kind of "hard knocking" method is indeed rare to hear in other provinces, but it is very common in Sichuan. (To be continued)

Outstanding Debt of the Jinpu Railway 58

Nanjing: The Jinpu Railway was originally built with British and German loans. It has suffered frequent military losses over the years, and its debt has increased significantly. The settlement at the end of December of the 21st year showed an outstanding debt of 184,294,800+ yuan in national currency, of which 136,167,000+ yuan belonged to assets, namely, the British and German loans. The rest is operating debt. The road's administrators decided in the 21st year to repay all debts. Among them, the total amount of loans from the five banks, originally agreed to be repaid, was 6.24 million yuan, which was scheduled to be repaid at 50,000 per month from January of the 22nd year to December of the 29th year, and at 60,000 per month from January of the 30th year to December of the 31st year. As of this month, the debt has been paid for 37 periods, totaling 1.65 million yuan in national currency. (26th, Special Dispatch)

Gao's bandits, numbering more than 200, have machine guns and raise the red flag. Representatives of Silverware Industry Petition in Beijing 60

Nanjing A delegation of over a hundred people from the National Silverware Industry Petition Group arrived in Beijing on the morning of the 26th. At 10 AM, they went to the Central Party Headquarters to petition for amendments to the silver usage regulations and to exempt them from restrictions on the silver content in their products. Secretary-General Ying received them and agreed to forward their petition to the chief secretary for review and instructions. At 11 AM, they went to the National Government, where Jiang Shenghuai was appointed to receive them. At 2 PM in the afternoon, they went to the Executive Yuan, where He Jizhi, the head of the Protocol Section, received them. At 3 PM, they went to the Ministry of Finance, where Dai Mingli, the Director of the Currency Department, and Liu Chengzheng received them. Dai agreed to forward their opinions to Minister Kong and also stated three points: 1. The regulations on the management of ornamental silver issued by the Ministry of Finance are based on the government's overall policy, and the silverware industry should understand this. 2. According to the Ministry of Finance's research, there is no technical obstacle to using 30% pure silver in the crafting of jewelry. 3. Silverware businesses are asked to strictly follow the silver content regulations stipulated by the Ministry of Finance and conduct thorough experiments. If the results show real difficulties, the silverware industry should draft a concrete plan based on the actual situation and submit it to the government for joint consultation, or a slight increase may be considered. At 4 PM, the entire group went to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum to pay their respects. At 6 PM, they attended a banquet hosted by the Beijing Silverware Industry Association. They returned to Shanghai that evening. (Special dispatch on the 26th)

Chinese Land Administration Society to Hold Annual Meeting in Hangzhou 69

The scope of discussion will include tenancy issues and the problems of aerial surveying versus manual surveying. Emphasis will also be placed on research reports from ordinary members and reports on the land administration situation from group members. Research reports from ordinary members include "The People's Livelihood View of History and Land Policy" by Huang Tongzhi, "The Grain Problem and the Land Problem in China" by Li Qing, "The Land Problem in Planned Economy" by Zhu Pingzhi, "The Tenancy System in Anhui" by Hong Ruijian, and "The Land Tax Reorganization in Zhejiang" by Wan Guoding, etc. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 26th)
