Disaster Relief Office in Hebei and Henan Provinces Requests Relief by Telegram

The Hebei Provincial Disaster Relief Office and the Henan Provincial Disaster Relief Office telegraphed: To the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Flood Relief in Various Provinces, Greetings. This is to inform you that the governments of Changyuan and Puyang counties in Hebei Province, and Huaxian County in Henan Province, have jointly issued an official letter stating: It has been found that the Changyuan Wenming Canal was created and repaired in the late Ming Dynasty, originating from Ninggangji in the north of the county seat and Liuqiao Village in the west of the city, merging into the Chen River in the northwest of the city, flowing north into Huaxian County, then named Liuqing River, passing through Huaxian County, flowing north into Puyang County, and finally flowing into the Yellow River. The canal runs through the three counties, with a total length of no less than 200 li, serving as a sluice gate for draining accumulated water in peacetime, and is of utmost importance to the livelihoods of the people in the three counties. More than 500 villages along the canal, with a population of more than 400,000, depend on the canal for survival. In recent years, the Yellow River has breached its banks, and the three counties have suffered severely from floods, leaving the people in dire straits. Moreover, the canal has been silted up by the water, and accumulated water has stagnated, making it impossible to drain. As a result, whenever there are continuous heavy rains, floods run rampant, inundating countless fields and crops. The direct and indirect losses amount to millions. In the summer and autumn of this year, incessant rains raged, and accumulated water formed rivers along the canal. The people of the three counties suffered the same fate as the flood victims. The damage was no different from the breaches of the Yellow River in previous years. After this devastating experience, we deeply feel that dredging this canal is not only an urgent and pressing task, but also a fundamental plan for the next century. However, due to consecutive years of disasters, the people's livelihood is in decline, and public and private resources are exhausted. Although we have the intention to dredge, we lack the ability to implement it. After painful reflection, learning from the past, we have thought about ways to prevent disasters and maintain the people's livelihood. We have consulted in detail and unanimously agreed that your association has always been concerned about the disaster victims in the three counties, has repeatedly provided relief, and has helped the people in distress. All living beings are grateful for your reconstruction. If the benefits and harms of dredging the canal and the plight of the disaster victims are described in detail to your association, we sincerely request that you allocate funds to provide work relief and preside over the dredging and repair. If you approve, both the national economy and the people's livelihood will benefit. It has been decided to prepare separate plans and submit them jointly by the three counties, drawing a complete map of the canal, and requesting your association to review and instruct, etc. It is recorded in the file. We respectfully observe that your association has a charitable heart and is very concerned about the welfare of the people. This righteous act concerns the water conservancy of the three counties, benefiting them once and for all, saving hundreds of millions of lives from water and fire, and putting them on a bed of safety. Although a one-time allocation of funds is relatively large, it is better to cure the disease than to treat the symptoms by repeatedly allocating relief funds, which is a passive remedy, patching up for a while. Therefore, we dare to jointly request and earnestly appeal, and earnestly request your association to consider the plight of the disaster area and provide special consideration, approving the allocation of funds to preside over the construction, so that the dredging and repair will be completed in the future, water conservancy will be greatly developed, and families will be prosperous. The people of the three counties will be grateful for your great kindness without end. Whether or not it is approved, we are submitting a plan and a complete map of the canal, and requesting you to forward them to your general association for review and discretionary allocation of funds for implementation. Attached is a canal dredging plan and a canal dredging plan map, etc. It has been found that the canals in the three counties are indeed the final outlets for draining accumulated water in the three counties, and dredging is indeed urgent. The proposed plan is also based on facts. However, the land price determined by Huaxian and Puyang counties for occupying civilian land, since it is an old canal, seems to have no need to use funds to purchase land again. Moreover, the proposed earthwork wages can also be discussed with local officials and gentry when implementing the project, and one-third or one-half of the civilian workers can be used to assist voluntarily to jointly complete the righteous act. It is still hoped that the conference will consider allocating funds for implementation. The Hebei Provincial Disaster Relief Office and the Henan Provincial Disaster Relief Office respectfully request, sincerely.

Yesterday's Negotiations with Representatives of the Special Zone Telephone Association Ended Without Results 104

Chinese and Western Directors to Temporarily Pilot

Refuse to Pay Fees and Await Removal

The Guowen News Agency reported that the Special Zone Telephone Issue Committee, in order to request the cancellation of the telephone price increase, sent representatives to negotiate with the Public Works Bureau yesterday afternoon, but without result. The committee is scheduled to convene another board meeting at 2 p.m. today to discuss the final response measures. The details are recorded as follows:

Sending Personnel to Negotiate Without Result

The Shanghai Telephone Company has announced new charging rules, which are scheduled to take effect on March 1. At a time when commerce is in decline and citizens cannot afford it, repeated appeals have been made to request the cancellation of this measure, but without result. After holding a joint meeting of user groups on the 20th of this month to discuss the final resistance measures, Zhang Yichen, Gu Wensheng, Li Kui, Ke Ganchen (substituting for Sheng Guren), and others were selected as representatives to negotiate with the Public Works Bureau. The representatives went to the Public Works Bureau yesterday afternoon and were received by General Manager Zhong Si and Associate Manager He De Kui. The representatives then proposed: The basic number of calls for commercial telephones should be increased to 333, and the basic number of calls for residential telephones should be increased to 217. If the quota is not met, the basic usage fee should be paid according to the Shanghai Telephone Company's announcement. The toll for calls between the special zone and the city should be cancelled. A meter should be installed next to each telephone. Zhong Si replied: The issue of increasing the basic number of calls, because this measure was proposed by the Chinese directors to organize a committee of experts to study, and Chinese expert Hu Ruixiang participated in the study, it cannot be changed again. Regarding the Chinese Concession toll, because the Ministry of Communications and the Shanghai Telephone Company have a temporary contract, it cannot be cancelled. Regarding the installation of meters, it will be submitted to the board of directors for discussion and may be accepted. The representatives believed that the replies were not satisfactory to the users, and the meeting ended at 3 p.m. without result.

Chinese and Western Directors Exchange Views

The Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Concession attaches great importance to the issue of telephone price increases in the special zone. It convened an executive committee last Saturday and decided on four measures, and sent letters to the Chinese directors attending the Public Works Bureau, Yu Qiaqing, Guo Shun, Xu Xinliu, Jiang Yiping, Xi Yushu, etc., to negotiate with the Public Works Bureau's board of directors. Yesterday morning at 10 a.m., the Chinese directors went to the Public Works Bureau and exchanged views with the Western directors attending the Public Works Bureau. As a result, the Western directors advocated that the new telephone system should be piloted for one year, while the Chinese directors advocated a pilot period of three months, but there was no formal meeting, so no decision was made.

Telephone Users Await Removal

The First Special Zone Citizens' Federation, regarding the issue of telephone price increases, has notified the sub-associations in each district to convene user meetings to discuss the entire plan. The association received reports from the fifth, twelfth, fifteenth, thirty-sixth, and thirtieth district sub-associations yesterday, stating: Regarding the telephone price increase, each district has expressed opposition. User conferences have been convened one after another, and it has been resolved that all users resolutely oppose the Shanghai Telephone Company's disregard for commercial difficulties and insistence on implementing the new charging system. It has now been decided that if the company implements the price increase from March, they will refuse to pay the fees and allow removal. They have already filled out voluntary forms and sent them to the Special Zone Telephone Issue Committee for reference, and notified all users to take uniform steps to achieve effectiveness.

Meeting Today to Discuss Measures

Opinions of the Banking Association's Subcommittee on Interest Rate Reduction 105

Guowen News Agency reported that since the Shanghai Banking Association and the Money Industry Association received instructions from the Ministry of Finance to discuss measures to reduce interest rates and submit them for review and handling, the Banking Association's subcommittee has drafted opinions. Yesterday, it also sought the opinions of the Money Industry Association, and it is said that a joint meeting is still needed to make specific decisions in order to submit them for review and handling. The situation yesterday is recorded as follows:

Glimpse of Opinions: The Banking Association's subcommittee, after holding a meeting to discuss, believes that reducing interest rates has a de facto chain relationship. If it is not thoroughly resolved, it is absolutely impossible to abandon the facts and talk emptily about reducing interest rates. For example, the interest rate on the troop reduction public debt is 6%, but in the past, the market price was always around 80 yuan per 100 yuan, so the interest rate was as high as 7% or more. Now, since the public debt law has changed, the market price is about 60 yuan per 100 yuan, which means that the interest rate has risen to about 10%. This has a chain relationship and must be resolved together. Secondly, since the currency system was improved on November 3 last year, the Central Bank has formed a bank of the banking industry. If the Central Bank does not first reduce interest rates and set interest rates on the signboard, simply holding commercial banks accountable is tantamount to closing the door and forcing them in, blocking the road and making them walk. This has a chain relationship and must be resolved first. Therefore, the subcommittee has submitted these opinions to the executive committee for discussion.

Seeking Opinions: Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Banking Association, called Qin Runqing, Qin Xiqing, and other leaders of the Money Industry Association yesterday afternoon, informing them that the Banking Association's subcommittee had drafted opinions and requesting the Money Industry Association to also put forward several opinions, so that a joint meeting of the banking and money industries could be convened on a regular basis to explore each other and make specific decisions for submission to the Ministry of Finance for review and handling.

Scheduling a Meeting: The Banking Association's subcommittee has already had all nine members, Pan Jiufen, Zhang Peishen, Ye Fuxiao, Zhang Naiqi, Zhang Jinglu, Zhang Wuyun, Yin Jichang, Zhang Zhuyu, and Luo Qinghua, sign the drafted opinions, which have been submitted to the executive committee for review. It is said that the subcommittee's mission can be said to be completed. Now, waiting for the association's chairman, Chen Guangfu, to set a date for the meeting, the executive committee meeting will be convened in the next few days.

Revised Measures for Punishing and Rewarding the Seizure of Illegally Transported Silver and Silver Coins 106

Ministry of Finance Requests Railways to Issue Circular for All Roads to Comply With

Railway Police Must Not Deliberately Obstruct and Disturb Passengers and Merchants

The Ministry of Railways approved the Ministry of Finance's consultation on the revised measures for punishing and rewarding the seizure of illegally transported silver and silver coins and issued a circular to all roads to comply with. The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations have been ordered to instruct the Transportation Department and the Police Department to comply. A reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency separately recorded the original order and measures below:

Railway Ministry Circular

The Ministry of Railways' Business Circular stated: Approved the Ministry of Finance's consultation Qianzi No. 2316 of January 31, approving your ministry's consultation Yezizi No. 173 of January 17, stating that the Jinpu Railway Bureau's submission requesting that a percentage of the seized illegally transported silver dollars be appropriated as rewards was submitted for verification and a reply was requested. Approved. The awarding of bonuses to those who contribute to the seizure of illegally transported silver coins and silver should be handled in accordance with the revised measures for punishing and rewarding the seizure of illegally transported silver and silver coins of this ministry. Approved the previous submission, and a copy of the aforementioned measures is enclosed for your information, and it is hoped that you will instruct your subordinate road bureaus to comply as a whole. A copy of the revised measures for punishing and rewarding the seizure of illegally transported silver and silver coins is attached for reference. Regarding the measures for applying for passports for transporting silver coins and silver and the punishment for illegally transporting and carrying them, all roads were instructed to comply on November 30, 24th year, Yezizi No. 4253. Now, in response to the Ministry of Finance's consultation on the measures for punishing and rewarding the seizure of illegally transported silver and silver coins, it concerns a circular, so it should be handled in accordance with the measures. However, railway police officers must not deliberately obstruct and disturb passengers and merchants on the pretext, hindering road operations and causing disputes. Approved the previous consultation, and the original document is being copied and issued, which you should immediately comply with. This order.

Reward and Punishment Measures

Revised Measures for Punishing and Rewarding the Seizure of Illegally Transported Silver and Silver Coins: Seizing silver coins or silver transported illegally without a permit shall be handled in accordance with Article 4 of the Measures for Applying for Passports for Transporting Silver Coins and Silver and the Punishment for Illegally Transporting and Carrying them. The confiscated silver coins or silver shall be sent to the Central, China, and Communications Banks to exchange for legal tender, and the bonus shall be distributed according to the following measures: (A) If the seizure is made independently by the customs or military police, the bonus shall be doubled in accordance with the customs' method of rewarding informants without inside connections, i.e., 60% for extraordinary merit and 40% for ordinary merit (for example, if 10,000 yuan of silver coins are smuggled and confiscated, military police or customs officers shall be awarded 6,000 yuan for extraordinary merit and 4,000 yuan for ordinary merit). (B) If the customs obtain an informant, the reward method is doubled, with military police and informants each receiving 40% and customs officers receiving 20% (as in the previous example, military police and informants each receive 4,000 yuan and customs officers receive 2,000 yuan). (C) If the military police obtain a tip-off from an informant and seize the goods as a result, the informant shall be awarded 60% and the military police shall be awarded 40%. (D) If the customs obtain a tip-off from an informant (without the assistance of military police) and seize the goods as a result, the informant shall be awarded 60% and the customs officers shall be awarded 40%. (E) If the customs seize the goods with the assistance of military police (without a tip-off from an informant), the military police shall be awarded 40% and the customs officers shall be awarded 40%. The name of the informant shall be kept confidential. Customs or military police seizing illegally transported silver coins and confiscating them, or sending cases to the court for treatment, shall report to the Ministry of Finance for verification on a monthly basis.

Gu Wensheng and Others Propose to the French Municipal Council to Add a Chinese Advisory Board System 107

Listing Five Major Reasons

When the French Concession Taxpayers' Association held its second executive committee meeting of this term, Executive Committee members Gu Wensheng and others urgently proposed that the French Concession Municipal Council should urgently add a Chinese Advisory Board system to improve municipal administration. The original text is recorded below: As an urgent proposal, the French Concession Municipal Council should urgently imitate the Public Concession, add a Chinese Advisory Board system to enhance Sino-French friendship, ease emotions, promote commerce, benefit municipal administration, and avoid misunderstandings and disputes. We believe that since the establishment of the Chinese Advisory Board by the Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession, Chinese and foreign opinions have merged harmoniously. They have cooperated and worked together to improve municipal administration and revitalize commerce, gradually eliminating obstacles. Both Chinese and foreigners have benefited from it, with small costs and significant results. It is a pity that the French Concession Municipal Council has not paid attention to this. Considering the performance, it is particularly inferior. Moreover, the French Concession area is prosperous and densely populated, comparable to the Public Concession. However, since previous years, it has been deeply affected by the recession, declining sharply. Looking at the surrounding areas, the city is desolate, and empty buildings are lined up, greatly reducing the Municipal Council's tax revenue, causing difficulties for both superiors and subordinates. Old stores have closed one after another, and entrepreneurs are even more reluctant to invest. Looking ahead at the commercial situation, it is getting worse. The people are living in poverty, and cases of committing crimes are heard daily. The courts are barely able to cope. Citizens occasionally commit minor oversights and are immediately punished. The ignorant bullies of the Vietnamese police force often abuse their power, using violence to oppress the citizens, seeking bribes, and disregarding commercial difficulties. Negative energy accumulates, leading to repeated disputes, and gradually becoming a breeding ground for sin. Furthermore, the cost of water and electricity in the French Concession is more expensive than in the Public Concession, cutting lines and stopping water, causing numerous disputes. The laws are harsh, leading to frequent detentions and fines, leaving people with almost no way to appeal. Merchants regard it as a daunting task, and complaints are rife, clearly showing the declining trend of the French Concession. There are inherent problems, which can be attributed to the authorities' lack of insight and the shortcomings of the municipal administration, which led to this situation. This is the first reason why it is urgent to add a Chinese Advisory Board system to revitalize the city. In the past, the French Concession Municipal Council often acted rashly in matters such as municipal facilities and tax increases, or was too hasty, building behind closed doors, causing many obstacles, and failing to actively help each other to achieve perfection. Currently, there are many aspects of the French Concession's municipal administration that need to be reformed, all requiring talent and funding, relying on Sino-foreign cooperation to widely solicit advice. This is the second reason why it is urgent to add a Chinese Advisory Board system to improve municipal administration. The lack of communication between the Municipal Council and the citizens has been a long-standing issue, leading to suspicion, misunderstandings, and other problems. This is inevitable. In the past, if citizens had good intentions or reasonable appeals, they were often restricted, like the relationship between Qin and Yue, making it difficult for lower-level opinions to reach the higher levels. It is difficult to expect the promotion of municipal administration to be beneficial. This is the third reason why it is urgent to add a Chinese Advisory Board system to eliminate misunderstandings. If the Municipal Council adds a Chinese Advisory Board, citizens' suggestions and contributions can be accepted by the Chinese Advisory Board and forwarded to the Municipal Council. If the Municipal Council has new policies to implement, it can consult with the Chinese Advisory Board to convey them to the citizens. From then on, mediation will be effective, and the work of coordination will be easily achieved. As a result, everything will be revived, and the effect of direct command will be achieved. It is only hoped that sincerity will prevail, avoiding alienation. Sincere hearts can melt mountain snow, and a handshake can thaw pond ice. With experienced guidance, it is easy to handle complex matters with simplicity and respond appropriately. This is the fourth reason why it is urgent to add a Chinese Advisory Board system for convenient communication. Recently, the authorities of the Public Concession have been quite aware of the times, able to uphold the overall situation. They have implemented measures to enhance the authority of Chinese employees in various institutions, selecting talented and capable individuals. In addition to adding a Chinese Advisory Board to the Municipal Council, the police department has also added a Chinese Deputy Chief Inspector, and there are Chinese district chiefs in various police stations. The relationship is harmonious, which is a great help. This is the general trend, and it is appropriate to adapt to the environment. Otherwise, what can a fish in the abyss hope for? Personnel changes are not immutable. This is the fifth reason why it is urgent to add a Chinese Advisory Board system to follow the trend. Considering the new additions in the Public Concession, there are many aspects. For the welfare of all citizens of our French Concession, it is necessary to add a Chinese Advisory Board system, making only the minimum requirement. For the Municipal Council, there is no risk of overstepping authority or wasting money. The estimated monthly cost is limited, but the benefits are many, greatly benefiting the citizens. This is truly the most important plan at present. Is this appropriate? We respectfully await your decision.

Guangdong Railway Bonds: Capital Repayment Method 110

The Guangdong-Hankou Railway bonds are being recalled and will be drawn and repaid annually starting from the 24th year of the Republic of China. The bond amount of 20 million yuan will be repaid evenly over 20 years, and will be paid off by the 43rd year of the Republic of China. Now, it has been announced by the National Government that it will be changed to drawing and repaying the principal annually from the 27th year of the Republic of China. The bond amount will be repaid evenly over 17 years and will still be repaid off by the 43rd year of the Republic of China.

From March 1st, China National Aviation Corporation Abolishes Air Zone System 112

Reduces Air Mail Rates

China National Aviation Corporation announced that to reduce the burden on the public and popularize airmail, the company will implement the abolition of the air zone system from March 1st of this year. All airmail letters sent to all parts of the country, regardless of distance, will be charged a uniform airmail fee of 25 cents per 20 grams, in addition to the ordinary postage of 5 cents. At the same time, the postage for air parcels, books, and printed matter will also be changed to a fee of 15 cents per 20 grams, regardless of distance. The company's current routes include: Shanghai-Ping Line: Shanghai, Nanjing, Haizhou, Qingdao, Tianjin, Beijing; Shanghai-Shu Line: Shanghai, Nanjing, Jiujiang, Hankou, Shashi, Yichang, Wanxian, Chongqing, Chengdu; Yu-Kun Line: Chongqing, Guiyang, Kunming; Shanghai-Yue Line: Shanghai, Wenzhou, Fuzhou, Xiamen, Shantou, Guangzhou; Yue-He Line: Guangzhou, Xiying, Hanoi for transfer to various European countries (for airmail sent from various parts of the country to Hanoi, the fee is 25 cents per 5 grams)

Construction of Cao'e River Bridge Commences on April 1st 113

Machinery and Materials Decided to Be Transported

Scheduled for Completion by National Day Next Year

The Cao'e River Bridge on the Hangzhou-Ningbo section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway had a steel and cement pier built in the early years of the Republic of China, but due to the sudden outbreak of the European War and the lack of required materials, the project was suspended midway. Since the new Minister of Railways, Zhang Jia'ao, took office, he deemed it necessary to complete the bridge and specially sent two engineers, Ma Zhicheng, to Shaoxing to prepare for the project. All application materials and machines have been transported in order by the procurement committee. The construction is now scheduled to commence on April 1st, with a completion deadline of next year's National Day.

Xu Gongdian, the judge of the First Special District Court, summoned both parties to investigate the matter and found it to be true. Yesterday afternoon, he announced the judgment in accordance with all the requests of the plaintiff.

Wei Haichen, a Criminal in the Case of Using Counterfeit Currency, Sentenced 118

Sentenced to Five Years in Prison

Since the Ministry of Finance issued new subsidiary coins on the 10th of this month, the public has found it convenient and exchanged them enthusiastically, with the supply falling short of demand. Therefore, the mint is working day and night to manufacture them. However, a group of unscrupulous people, ignorant of the law and disregarding the consequences, secretly forged lead-nickel coins in the dark, used them in the market, and disrupted the financial order. On the morning of the 23rd of this month, Yuan Xinzhong, a Chinese detective from the Putuo Road Police Station, arrested a Jiangbei man named Wei Haichen at the intersection of Roberts Road and Xiaoshadu Road, who was found to be carrying 120 counterfeit ten-cent coins made of lead. Then, according to Wei's confession, he and the French police detectives went to No. 6, Lane 455, Kangti Road, and busted a counterfeiting machine, and found 10 counterfeit coins of the aforementioned type, as well as plaster powder, lead blocks, stoves, and other items. The Jiangbei man Zhang Yuxiang, who was making the coins, and Zhang Baoshan were also taken back to the police station and sent to the First Special District Court. The details of the interrogation have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Liu Yugua, a judge, continued the interrogation in the Eighth Criminal Court. First, Zhang Tianyin, the police lawyer, stated that in order to clarify the truth in this case during the adjournment, he had ordered the defendant Zhang Yuxiang to manufacture the coins according to law in the police station. He purchased some plaster powder, made a model, and poured in the lead blocks that had been seized. However, due to the short time, the plaster powder was not dry, and perhaps there were other things in the lead blocks, so the coins made were blurred. Later, the police remelted the 10 counterfeit coins that had been seized and made several coins, which had clear patterns and were lifelike. Therefore, Zhang Yuxiang was the manufacturer, and Wei Haichen and Zhang Baoshan were the users. He then presented the counterfeit coins to the case. After Liu questioned the three defendants again, he ruled in court that Wei Haichen intended to use counterfeit general subsidiary coins and deliver them to others, and sentenced him to five years of imprisonment. The 120 counterfeit subsidiary coins were confiscated. Zhang Yuxiang and Zhang Baoshan were transferred to the Shanghai Second Special District Local Court for trial due to improper jurisdiction.

Shen Zhonglian Commits Suicide with a Hunting Rifle 120

Shen Served in the Police Force for Twenty Years

Retired Last Year and Suddenly Became Pessimistic

Shen Zhonglian, a 48-year-old man from Zhenhai, Zhejiang, who lived at No. 5, Bei Yongtai Lane, Kangnao Road, once worked in the Shanghai Public Concession Police Department for 20 years. He accumulated merits and was promoted to the position of deputy detective. In the spring of last year, Shen suddenly resigned and retired to live at home. However, because he had no savings, he soon became panicked. Although he wanted to find another job, he never succeeded. Therefore, Shen often showed pessimism, but those around him thought that Shen's personality was very strong, and that he was only temporarily depressed, so they did not pay attention. Who knew that at about 2:00 p.m. yesterday, Shen took advantage of his family's unpreparedness and privately used a hunting shotgun to commit suicide in his room with live ammunition. At that time, his family suddenly heard a gunshot coming from Shen's bedroom and rushed to investigate. They saw Shen lying stiffly on the ground, with fresh blood overflowing from his chest, flowing all around. A shotgun was left beside him, and the smell of gunpowder filled the room. He was dead. They quickly reported to the police station, who sent detectives to investigate and immediately transported the body to the autopsy station to await a report to the court for verification.

工部局 Intelligence Office, Last Year's Work Report 121

Since the establishment of the Public Concession's Intelligence Office, its workload has increased daily. News releases sent to various newspapers in this city, with the exception of those occasionally not published due to insufficient space, have generally been adopted by both Chinese and foreign newspapers. This is because the news from the office is largely prepared in advance, decided upon by the Board of Directors, or deemed suitable for disclosure by the highest authorities before being immediately released. Therefore, the news is extremely timely, and the staff members have served in the news industry for many years. As a result, the writing style of the releases is well-suited to the needs of newspapers, and editors can use them directly. The office issues releases daily in three languages: English, Chinese, and Japanese, with the three heads of each language section responsible for their respective areas. In 1935, the office issued a total of 455 English releases, 490 Chinese releases, and 450 Japanese releases. The Chinese releases were generally published by various newspapers.

In addition to the regular writing and issuing of news releases, the Chinese and Japanese sections of the Intelligence Office translate news and commentary published in newspapers that are related to the Public Concession and its administrative facilities into English. These translations are then sent to the relevant authorities for reference and adoption. The importance of this work has become increasingly evident. On significant municipal issues, such as the telephone problem, the Chinese section head translated no fewer than seventy newspaper editorials and news articles into English last year. Regarding issues like the rickshaw problem, approximately sixty news reports were translated. The total number of translated articles was about 300.

Chinese Buddhist Association's Proposal Regarding Temple Registration: Suggestion for Local Buddhist Associations to Coordinate 125

The Chinese Buddhist Association states that the nationwide general registration of temples has been promulgated by the Ministry of Interior, with rules issued to all provinces for implementation. However, the registration forms are detailed and precise, and filling them out would be extremely difficult for those without knowledge of the form. Previously, during the registration of temples in various provinces between 1928 and 1929, many abbots of temples, unfamiliar with the filling-out procedures, often paid others to fill them out on their behalf. When submitted to the government offices, they were often returned for re-filling due to non-compliance with procedures, with many repeated trips still not resolving the issues. There were also cases where government offices sternly urged compliance, but the forms could not be submitted. The pain felt by the abbots of various temples was indescribable. If proper measures are not planned for this general registration of temples, disputes and difficulties will inevitably ensue. Therefore, a request was submitted to the Ministry of Interior to issue orders to all provinces to allow local Buddhist branches to select suitable personnel to coordinate with the personnel in charge of registration at the handling agencies at any time, and to guide the abbots of various temples in filling out the forms according to the regulations, so as to achieve proper results and avoid obstacles. The Ministry of Interior has now approved and issued orders to all provinces to act accordingly.

Yangtze River Imports: Change of Anchorage Sand Buoy 128

Navigation Notice No. 1080 of the Maritime Department of the Inspectorate General of Customs states: It has been found that the various buoys in the import area of the South Channel of the Yangtze River under the Jianghai Customs have been added or moved for the convenience of dredging projects. The Bureau has announced this in Navigation Notice No. 1071. It is now found that the dredging area of ​​the Yangtze River import intercepting sand will be changed. All the buoys there should be cancelled or added accordingly to facilitate the progress. The cancellation, addition, and implementation dates of the various buoys are listed below. All shipping merchants are to be informed accordingly. This is a special announcement. The details are as follows: A. Buoys to be cancelled: Dredging First Buoy and Dredging Second Buoy; B. Buoys to be added: Dredging Seventh Buoy, which is a light buoy, yellow on top and black on the bottom, equipped with an alternating red light, flashing once every eight seconds, that is, flashing on and off for four seconds each. From the location of the establishment, the true north of Nanhui is 236.5 degrees, at a distance of 7.18 nautical miles. This buoy is set to indicate the northern side of the dredging area and is not for navigational signs; Dredging Eighth Buoy, which is a light buoy, decorated in red, equipped with an alternating white light, flashing once every eight seconds, that is, flashing on and off for four seconds each. This buoy setting is to indicate the right side of the waterway for upstream vessels. From the location of the establishment, the true north of Nanhui is 237.25 degrees, at a distance of 6.92 nautical miles; C. Implementation date: Around March 2nd of this year. There will be no further announcement at that time; D. Related charts: Hydrographic Chart Nos. 505 and 1011 of the Ministry of the Navy of the Republic of China.

Page 13

Yang Runde of Treasure Department Submits to Ministry, Requests Establishment of Central Credit Agency 129

Advocates for Securitization of Collateral

To Facilitate Stagnant Situation

Shenshi News reports that Mr. Yang Runde, manager of the securities department of Shanghai Commercial and Savings Bank, believes that due to poor management and improper operations of industrial and commercial organizations in our country, even though there is abundant idle capital in society, the business sector still cannot expect assistance from capitalists. Therefore, he advocates for the securitization of collateral to alleviate the current stagnant situation. However, to gain the trust of investors, it is necessary to establish a central credit agency so that all parties can clearly understand the actual situation of the business sector, and then dare to invest boldly. Below is the text of his submission to the Ministry of Industry: Regarding the submission of a request to establish a central credit agency to investigate the actual conditions of companies in order to facilitate the circulation of company shares. The reason why industry and commerce in our country are not developed is that the shortage of capital is the main reason, and the stagnation of company securities and the inability of funds to circulate are the problems. Even if there is abundant idle capital in the country, it is still difficult to expect investment concepts to develop. The reason is that the Chinese people lack trust in enterprises. The key to the problem lies in poor management, the lack of a precise system, the adherence to traditional business practices, the lack of transparency in accounting, and the inappropriate distribution of personnel, forming a monopoly. Under this kind of environment, except for a few well-organized commercial organizations, few dare to invest. Take the Shanghai foreign merchant companies as an example. Years ago, funds were accumulated in the city, and the money market was ample. The issuance of corporate bonds by Shanghai Electric Power Company, Shanghai Telephone Company, Public Works Bureau, and Zhonghe Real Estate Company amounted to several million yuan one after another. Subscribers flocked in, and in a blink of an eye, the quota was full. On the other hand, when our country's industry and commerce are in a precarious state, it is difficult to hope that those with surplus capital will lend a helping hand even with painstaking support. The only way out is to apply to the banking industry for loans with factories, bases, and goods as collateral. The interest rates are high and the debts are heavy, and it is difficult for the banking industry to bear the burden. Therefore, domestic insightful people advocate for the securitization of collateral to alleviate the current stagnant situation. For example, real estate collateral is changed to the method of mortgage bonds to unclog the market. In fact, the Shanghai Stock Exchange only auctions national bonds, and brokers occasionally buy and sell company shares, but this is just a decoration on the market. The profits are not as high as those of government bonds, so it is inevitable that brokers will choose one over the other. Recently, the authorities of the exchange decided to promote the trading of shares to support the development of industry. It is planned to start with public utilities first, and then other industries. In advance, the exchange should consult with each company for consent. Letters were sent to each company, totaling 150 copies, asking them to select the best performers among companies with capital, public reserve, assets, liabilities, and business conditions for auction as a trial. Only thirteen or four companies responded. It is the practice of Chinese companies not to disclose internal information to outsiders. Although the establishment of the China Credit Investigation Agency can conduct detailed investigations, it is difficult to obtain accurate information because companies cannot be open and honest. Banking institutions tighten loan disbursements based on this. Therefore, the establishment of a central credit agency is an urgent task. However, at this time of financial difficulties, it may be difficult to set up a special agency. First cooperate with the China Credit Investigation Agency to make up for the shortcomings. Your Ministry is in charge of investigating national industries, and it is easy to unify domestic commercial organizations. Every six months or a year, order them to fill out balance sheets, profit and loss statements, property catalogs, and business status reports, and to check the facts at any time. The stock exchange can ask the credit agency about the actual situation at any time to determine the merits of the shares. Investors also have something to follow, and the future of the industry can develop on the right track. At this time, when the foreign merchant stocks of the Shanghai Public Industry Association are in decline, and the government is unifying government bonds to eliminate speculation, we are given the opportunity to develop domestic industrial securities. I humbly submit my opinion, and I hope that it is appropriate. I should report to your office for review, approval, and compliance, which would be in the public interest.

Ningbo Industrial Bank Intensifies Resumption of Business, Depositors with Unknown Addresses Can Collect Directly, Moving to Shanxi Road Office on March 5th 139

Since the Ningbo Industrial Bank's recovery office began issuing 20% ​​of cash to long-term depositors, the procedures have been cumbersome and there are many depositors, so it takes a long time. It is now learned that the savings portion will be completed soon, and the commercial portion has also been issued since the 1st of this month. However, due to the sluggish market situation, it is not easy to raise cash. It has been agreed that whether it is commercial time deposit or special current, those under 5 yuan will be fully taken, those between 5 yuan and 40 yuan will take 20%, and those above 40 yuan will take 20%, 30% of the two-year term deposit certificate, and 50% for stock. This method is also a better way for the preparatory office to seek a solution when it is impossible to prevent depositors from suffering losses. In fact, the organization of the office is half composed of depositors, feeling the pain of their own. Hoping that the bank will have the possibility of development after its resumption of business, until today, the commercial depositors have been able to understand the difficulty of the office and are happy to accept it. The office's method of withdrawing money requires a letter. It is found that a few commercial depositors have sent letters to notify them, either because of relocation or because the address is unknown, which has delayed the date of disbursement. It is now planned to invite commercial depositors with unknown addresses to collect directly without waiting for the announcement, so as to be quick. It is also heard that the preparatory office will renew the lease of the general office address with the landlord in order to save expenses, and is scheduled to move to the second floor of the general office at No. 142 Shanxi Road (Nanjing Road) from March 5th, and will continue to work as usual.

Record of the Li-Chiao Commemoration Meeting 146

The Shanghai Li-Chiao United Association held a commemoration meeting yesterday for the sixth anniversary of the revocation of the ban on Li-Chiao. Zhang, Chen, Pu Yusheng, and Dai Jinyong were publicly elected as the presidium. Chairman Zhang first reported that Li-Chiao has a public hall, which was first established in Tianjin by Elder Master Yin and is now called the West Elder Public Hall (the site of the Tianjin Li-Chiao United Association). Subsequently, branches were established in various provinces, and there are now more than 9,000 public halls. In addition to encouraging people to quit bad habits, charitable and public welfare undertakings are also carried out. Those who join the religion must abide by the teachings of past masters, learn tolerance, learn to take losses, learn loyalty and honesty, and learn peace as principles. Therefore, Li-Chiao followers are respected, and religious affairs are so developed. In 1925, Yichen and others found that the religion was not unified, being called Li Shan, Li Men, and Li Dao with inconsistent names. It should be corrected to Li-Chiao, and a united association was organized. In 1929, the Jiangsu Provincial Party and Government organs banned Li-Chiao with great force. Representatives from various public halls came to the association to request assistance. Yichen petitioned the central government to revoke the ban. On February 26, 1930, the Ministry of Interior issued a notice, stating in brief that it had received Executive Yuan Order No. 736, which forwarded the Central Party Department's order regarding the ban on Li-Chiao. The Jiangsu Provincial Party Department was instructed to revoke the resolution banning Li-Chiao, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government was also instructed to revoke the ban and inform all parties concerned. Thus, such a large storm was calmed. If not for the efforts of this association, Li-Chiao would have been completely destroyed. Subsequently, Pu Yusheng, Liao Shouchong, Dai Jinyong, and others delivered speeches in succession, encouraging the members. The meeting then discussed the matter of the China National Li-Chiao United Association and adjourned.

Sanitary Conditions in the Public Concession Last Month 150

According to the report of the Head of the Health Department of the Public Works Department, although the mortality rate of residents in the Public Concession increased significantly in January of this year, the cause was not due to infectious diseases. Due to the abolition of the Lunar New Year and the cold weather this month, only over five thousand one hundred people were vaccinated in the concession. However, smallpox still breaks out from time to time. Anyone who has not been properly vaccinated in the past three years should be vaccinated as soon as possible to prevent unforeseen circumstances.

Furthermore, during the Lunar New Year, the candies sold in various shops are often dyed in red and green colors. The Health Department tested no less than 600 kinds of these candies, and found that about 6% of them contained toxic lead pigments, which are harmful to consumption. After the Health Department has investigated, warned, and called for inspections of this habit every year, it has gradually decreased, and residents are becoming increasingly aware of the harm to health. Therefore, it has not been heard that anyone has become seriously ill from eating them.

In terms of vital statistics, a total of 104 foreign babies were born, of which 93 lived in the Public Concession, including 48 male babies and 45 female babies. A total of 1,030 Chinese babies were reported to be born, of which 989 lived within the concession, including 529 male babies and 460 female babies. A total of 54 foreign residents died, the greatest cause of death being pulmonary tuberculosis, pneumonia, and heart disease. The mortality rate of Chinese residents was over 15 per thousand, the greatest causes of death being old age, pulmonary tuberculosis, bronchitis, and heart disease.

Letter to the Editor 153

To the esteemed chief editor of the Shenbao: After reading your newspaper's report on the Datongxing Steamship Company refusing to provide relief to the Tongshun crew members, the content was inaccurate. After investigation, the Tongshun vessel of our company ran aground in Hainan Island on February 8th. The first group of 38 crew members arrived in Shanghai on the 20th, and the second group of 25 arrived on the 24th. The luggage of the first group of people was all brought down with them. Except for the luggage of the compradors and accounting staff, which were stored in the company, the rest was loaded onto a moving company's car and sent to the hotel. When the second batch of crew members disembarked, their luggage was all handed over to the hotel to pick up. In total, there were 25 crew members, and the Ping An Hotel picked up 43 pieces of luggage, excluding the parts they brought with them. I ask, is the luggage of our crew members as reported in your newspaper completely lost? In good conscience, I am afraid it is difficult to answer. Except for the captain, all the crew members have arrived. Our company issued full salaries for February, and the senior crew members, such as the first mate, second mate, third mate, radio operator, first engineer, second engineer, and third engineer, all received their salaries without any problem. In addition, 17 compradors and accounting staff members also received their salaries and went home. However, out of compassion for the small number of lower-level crew members, our company, even in these days of declining shipping industry and difficult to support, still gave each person a subsidy of five yuan. Those who wanted to go home were also helped to find a boat. In terms of conscience, our company feels that it has nothing to be ashamed of to the lower-level crew members. However, these people still run around and publish one-sided accounts in the newspapers. Our company has always admired the chief editor for upholding justice and should publicize the true situation in the newspapers to avoid confusion. The so-called refusal of our company to provide relief to the Tongshun crew members is actually that the crew members not only have no losses, as mentioned above, but also of course there is no relief to speak of. The crew members expect too much, and our company is currently experiencing extremely severe business decline, which is difficult to accept. The matter is as scheduled, and should therefore ask the chief editor to correct it. Respectfully, the Datongxing Steamship Company, February 26th.

The Paraffin Wax Industry in Shanghai (Continued) 155

— Chief Editor of China Credit

(Summary of Shanghai Industry and Commerce XV)

3. Sales of Paraffin Wax and Foreign Wax

Sales of imported paraffin wax are divided into candle making and soap making. This has been mentioned earlier. Jiangsu and Zhejiang have dense populations and more financial resources, and Shanghai is an industrial center with many soap factories. Therefore, the sales in these two provinces account for almost half of the national production. The next largest are Guangdong and Fujian, where the uses are also extensive. Other provinces have less demand. The sales channels, both domestic and foreign, are described below.

Foreign Sales — Paraffin wax sales to foreign countries were once not weak. According to the export figures for 1912, the amount reached 214,349 piculs, valued at 2,333,759 taels of Customs Silver. Afterwards, the amount decreased year by year. Although Shanghai export firms occasionally asked oil firms for sample prices, no transactions were made. The table below shows the export amount for the past three years.

Domestic Sales — Domestic sales mainly consist of wax from Heben, Xiaoxi, Pingyou, Jinshi, Chongjing. Sales depend on the work of Taoist rituals. It is found that the Taoist rituals period is from March to May, called the summer Taoist rituals; August to October, called the autumn Taoist rituals; November to December, called the winter Taoist rituals. The summer and winter rituals use the most oil. Therefore, domestic sales are also the strongest at this time. In recent years, the decline of the social economy and the rise of the anti-superstition movement have greatly affected domestic sales. There are currently 110 candle shops in Shanghai, with an annual consumption of over 50,000 piculs.

Soap Sales — Paraffin wax soap factory sales have been greatly affected by the dumping of Shandong beef tallow, Singapore coconut oil, and Japanese hardened oil for many years. Since the price of paraffin wax has fallen, imports have decreased. Taking coconut oil imports as an example, it was 57,574 metric tons in 1933, which decreased to 53,776 metric tons in 1934, and further decreased to 22,415 metric tons in 1935. The decreasing trend of coconut oil has helped the development of paraffin wax sales. It is found that the peak period for paraffin wax soap sales is from February to May. Sales fall during the autumn and winter. In recent years, major soap factories often stockpile goods in winter, so winter sales have also turned around.

The main sales of white wax are also for candles and Taoist rituals, used to cover the candle surface (commonly known as "covering red"). In addition, it is also used to make wax pills, wax paper, etc. Chinese tea exported to the Philippines is also made with white wax. In 1912, exports reached 3,764 piculs. Today, it is getting worse every day. The export amount for the past three years is shown in the table below.

Domestic sales are also declining. Since the import of foreign wax, foreign wax has been used to replace it for covering candle surfaces. The other usage is very small. The annual consumption in Shanghai is 3,500 piculs, with rice core accounting for the majority.

To clarify the sales figures for paraffin wax and white wax, the consumption amounts in various regions are listed below.

The import of foreign wax began in 1905. At that time, there were no foreign wax factories in our country. After the Mobil Oil Company sold it, the Gao Yuxing Candle Shop in Nanshi first tried it, and the effect was very good. In 1919, Asia Texaco took over the distribution, and other import and export firms also followed suit. In April 1934, the Assistance Society transported Russian wax to Shanghai, and the import value increased greatly. Currently, the dealers of foreign wax in Shanghai include Mobil, Asia, Texaco, Tianxiang, Kongshi, Gongli, and the Assistance Society. The sales method is mostly direct orders from users to foreign firms. In the past three years, the import amount was 261,923 metric tons in 1933, 263,499 metric tons in 1934, and 306,633 metric tons in 1935. The annual value is over 8 million national currency. (To be continued)

Sports News

Record of Xu Chengji's Miserable Defeat in the Philippines 156

After Winning Two Sets, He Lost Two Sets and Retired: Chinese and Foreign Spectators in the Philippines Expressed Dissatisfaction with Xu

Wang Wenzheng Continues to Win, with Excellent Public Opinion

(Manila Airmail Special Dispatch) Xu Chengji, our country's tennis champion who traveled a long distance, made his debut yesterday at the All-Philippine International Tennis Championship. After winning two sets, he actually retired midway, causing the unknown Filipino player Royales to win the final victory, greatly disappointing the expectations of Chinese and foreign spectators on the scene.

Xu Chengji Gives Up the Victory

Yesterday was the third day of the competition. Due to the reputation of Xu Chengji and Wang Wenzheng's decisive battle against the Far Eastern University's expert Pulingdan, a large number of people flocked to the stadium to watch the game, mostly overseas Chinese. Xu's opponent was the unknown Royales W.K., who was not on the list of the top ten tennis players in the Philippines. However, after the match, Xu was greatly out of shape. Although he won the first two sets with 7-5 and 7-5, each set had to go through multiple deuces to win. After the third set started, Xu protested to the umpire about the boundary line when he was leading with a score of 3-2, stopping the game for more than ten minutes. Later, for some unknown reason, Xu voluntarily gave the entire set victory to his opponent. The umpire then ruled that Royales won the third set with a score of 6-3. Afterwards, both sides moved from the first tennis court to the central court to continue the game. Royales then won the fourth set with a score of 6-1. Since both sides had won two sets each, the outcome depended on the fifth set. When Royales took the lead with a score of 1-0, Xu suddenly suffered a cramp and fell to the ground, so he voluntarily retired. Royales luckily won again. As a result, Royales won the final victory with a score of 5-7, 5-7, 6-3, 6-1, and 1-0 (the result of the fifth set before the end of the game).

Great Disappointment for Chinese and Foreign Spectators

It is found that Xu's decision to perform disappointed the spectators. There was much discussion in the audience. Some said that when Xu was leading with a score of 3-2 in the third set, he did not continue to fight, but instead gave up the victory, which was both lacking in fighting spirit and lost the purpose of sports. Others said that even if the umpire and line judge were biased at the time, Xu should have endured and fought, so as not to lose the true color of a sportsman. Still others said that according to the rules, a player who retires midway is considered a failure. Xu's retirement midway in the third set meant that he could not continue the game. Even if he won in the fifth set, he should have been considered a failure according to the rules.

Wang Wenzheng Shows Great Power

Among the various matches yesterday, the most exciting performance and the strongest momentum should be attributed to Wang Wenzheng, our country's tennis expert. Wang's opponent yesterday was Pulingdan, the tennis star of Far Eastern University. This person's tennis skills are extraordinary. In this year's All-Philippine University Tennis League, he once defeated the Philippine tennis king, Dagavia. Wang Wenzheng's match against him yesterday was no different from the first hurdle to enter the semi-finals. Pulingdan also knew that Wang Wenzheng was one of the dangerous figures in this year's competition. Pulingdan first won the first set with a score of 6-3. Wang won the second and third sets in a row. Pulingdan then tried to cheer up and won back the fourth set with a score of 6-4. After the two heroes each won two sets, they made a final decisive battle. Wang Wenzheng took this as the key to victory, and with the cheers of the overseas Chinese to cheer him on, he showed great power in the continued battle, using his accurate left and right shots and net-rushing blocking skills to defeat the enemy with a score of 6-1. The overall result was 3-6, 6-0, 6-1, 4-6, and 6-1. Wang won the semi-final qualification in the cheers of the entire venue. He will play in the semi-finals against the Australian Hash tomorrow (15th). Judging from the two players' results in the past few days, Wang is expected to overwhelm the Australian player.

Wang Wenzheng Gains Great Praise

Wang Wenzheng has gained quite a bit of praise in the Philippines. The Overseas Chinese Commercial News commented on Wang, "Wang Wenzheng, our country's tennis champion, came to the Philippines to compete and defeated the Philippine singles champion, Gavia, to win the Manila Municipal Tennis Championship. He was retained by the Philippine Sports Promotion Association and is now participating in the Philippine International Tennis Competition. It can be said that Wang's contribution has made Filipinos recognize the progress of our country's tennis skills. The victory or defeat on the court is a common occurrence for athletes. When we criticize athletes, we should certainly not only value victory. An athlete's attitude and personality are actually more important than victory or defeat, because cultivation must take care of both body and mind. If only power and skill are emphasized, and nothing else is asked, it is true that the true meaning of sports is lost. Wang's good tennis skills are needless to say. His attitude and personality have things that are worthy of our attention. First, he is a calm person. His demeanor is extremely calm. Second, he absolutely does not have the frivolous and arrogant bad habits of ordinary athletes. Every move and every action shows his honest nature. Third, he is good at taking care of himself and has no habits that harm his body and mind. Fourth, no matter who the opponent is, and no matter what the outcome is, he tries his best to play his ball, never letting up for a moment, and never being sloppy for a step. He is not only like this during the competition, but also during ordinary practice. This spirit is the most rare. This is the secret of his success, and it is also the secret of all other successful people." (Manila, 14th)

Participation in the World Games Simple Modifications to the National Arts Preliminary 158

Weightlifting Not to Exceed Four Performers Modified to Six

It has been decided to participate in the World Games weightlifting competition, and the number of national arts performance athletes are four weightlifters, and six for national arts performances. In order to select truly talented individuals to produce these ten athletes, the selection committee has sent letters from the All-China Sports Federation to the education departments of all provinces and cities, as well as national arts centers, to select and recommend outstanding individuals. The initial quota for recommendation was set at no more than four people. After receiving the notice, each region actively proceeded. However, in each unit, there were special developments in weightlifting and national arts talents. If the limit was only four people, it would be difficult to avoid regrets in the future, so a request was made to expand the recommendation quota. Now, the selection committee has adopted the opinion and modified the recommendation clause in the selection rules. It is now stipulated that the recommendation quota for each unit should not exceed four for weightlifting and six for national arts performances. In addition to being published in various newspapers, the association has also sent letters to various units. The selection is divided into preliminary selection and re-selection. The date is in early May, and the location is in Shanghai. As for the selection method, it has not yet been specifically discussed. Four major weightlifters will be chosen, one from each level. This is because weightlifting is divided into light, light-heavy, medium, and light-heavyweight levels. The person with the highest combined score in the snatch and clean and jerk in each level will be considered qualified. Six national arts performance athletes will be selected. The procedure for this selection is more complicated, but the only standard for selection is the one with the most exquisite and extensive skills. Other qualifications of the athlete, such as physique, attitude, and academic knowledge, are also important conditions for selection. The Sports Association announced yesterday that in the preliminary selection rules for participating in the World Games weightlifting competition and the national arts performance, Article 5, the recommendation item, states that each provincial and municipal unit may apply for an increase in the quota due to special circumstances. Therefore, the selection committee has modified it as follows: The recommendation quota for each provincial and municipal education department or each provincial and municipal national arts center to recommend to Shanghai to participate in the preliminary selection shall not exceed four for weightlifting and six for national arts performances. (Note: The original text stated that the quota for each unit should not exceed West).

Shandong Province's 4th National Arts Provincial Examination Scheduled for April 15th 160

(Jinan, 26th) The 4th National Arts Provincial Examination is scheduled to be held on April 15th, with a budget of 10,000 yuan.

Jinan Correspondence: According to the regulations of the Central National Arts Hall, each provincial National Arts Hall should hold a provincial examination every year. However, in recent years, not many provinces have actually implemented such examinations. Shandong has always had many strong athletes, and the practice of national arts has long been widespread among the people. Since Han Fuqu, the chairman of the provincial government, also took the post of director of the National Arts Hall, he has worked even harder to promote it, with remarkable results. All military units and county militia and public security bureaus, etc., all regard national arts as a necessary subject. National Arts Halls have been widely established in various places, and talented individuals have emerged to take on guidance roles. The provincial National Arts examination is held once a year and has already been held three times. The first and second-class athletes who have been selected have participated in the National Games and the North China Games, achieving outstanding results. Now that winter is over and spring is here, and the ice and snow are gradually melting, preparations should be made to hold the 4th provincial examination to select talent. Han Fuqu personally instructed Bao Laigeng, the deputy director of the National Arts Hall, yesterday to start preparing everything immediately. Furthermore, in order to select top-notch national arts talent, he intends to have male and female athletes who have been ranked in the first class in previous provincial examinations re-register and participate in the examination. Also, in the past, in order to popularize national arts, he issued an order to all counties to establish county National Arts Halls, with the county magistrate concurrently serving as the director. For the position of deputy director, Chairman Han ordered the assignment of specialized personnel skilled in national arts. Therefore, it was decided that the deputy directors of the National Arts Halls in all counties should also be ordered to come to the province to participate in the 4th provincial examination, in order to select talent. The budget for the conference is already on file and should not be a problem. It is also planned to expand the scale of the event compared to previous years. After receiving the instructions, Bao Laigeng immediately began preparing everything. Recently, the Preparatory Committee for the 4th Provincial Examination was established first, and all regulations and the date of the conference will be decided by the Preparatory Committee, and so on.

Educational News

After Professor Liu Kan'yuan's Arrest, the Beiping Student Unrest Has Gradually Eased 167

As many as 109 students have been arrested. Leading figures have secretly left Beiping, and the Student Union is not active.

Tsinghua professors resume teaching, requesting original students to be given three major demerits.

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The student unrest at various universities in Beiping has gradually eased because the military and police authorities ordered secret agents to first investigate the reactionary elements in each school, and then dispatched a large number of military and police to search the universities, arresting as many as 109 students. Currently, students who love activities in various schools have safely returned to class. Liu Kan'yuan, a well-known professor in Beiping, was arrested at his private residence on the 24th. Today, reactionary elements secretly left Beiping one after another. After the president admonished the students, the unrest at Tsinghua University also calmed down today (the 25th). The details of the situation in various parties are recorded below.

Reasons for Professor Liu's Arrest

Liu Kan'yuan is a professor at China College, a lecturer at National Normal University, and a lecturer at the Faculty of Law and Commerce of Beiping University. He is a 42-year-old from Xiangyin, Hunan, with a master's degree in political science from the Imperial University of Japan. He has a profound research on the theories of political economy, and his theories are novel. The old-school professors oppose him, and there are many students in various schools who support Liu. Liu's lectures on social science are welcomed by the majority of students, and students also use Liu's radical views and approach him a lot. It is rumored that Liu is a member of the Third Party, but according to those close to Liu, this is not true. Yang Likui, a Standing Committee member of the Joint Association of Faculty and Staff of Tianjin Colleges and Universities, responded to the third point of the Student Union's three letters of inquiry: "Last December, a professor openly spoke in the Faculty of Arts of the Normal University about the need for a revolution of farmers and workers. The next day, someone told me that a certain professor did this because he was opposed by students for teaching, so he made such radical remarks to win the favor of young people. Seeing that he didn't play the red middle card after someone deducted it, and couldn't win three times, he was so angry that he couldn't sleep for two nights. Can such a person make a revolution? Isn't this propaganda reactionary and deceiving students?" When the Beiping authorities read the newspaper, they realized that there were indeed people in the university professors who incited student unrest. After investigation, Liu was arrested. When Liu was arrested, Liu happened to be at his private residence at No. 11, Nan Banbi Street, Shibalijie. After the military police entered the room, they immediately tied Liu with hemp rope and sent him to the Public Security Bureau. Liu's attitude was calm. After arriving at the Public Security Bureau, he was interrogated several times and is still under investigation for evidence. Liu's wife took clothes and food to the bureau today to visit Liu, but was not allowed to meet him. Only the clothes and food were left and transferred to Liu by the mountain police.

Student Movement Has Stopped

After Professor Liu's arrest, students from Tsinghua University, Yenching University, Peking University, and China College who were involved in student movements secretly left Beiping one after another. The members and staff of the Student Union refused to see guests, and various publications also stopped indefinitely. At this point, the Beiping student movement has once again entered a state of rest. Among the 43 students who were previously arrested at Northeastern University, there were two female students who were very talented. It is said that someone falsely accused them. Students Chuan Xian, Wan Jiadong, Ren Qingyu, and Dong Xigong from Jingye English Night School were arrested again today. Many students from Municipal No. 1 Middle School and No. 1 Girls' Middle School have been arrested. A total of 109 students from various universities have been arrested one after another, and most of them are unknown.

Tsinghua Student Unrest Has Subsided

Tsinghua University students demanded exemption from examinations, and the professors resigned in anger, causing a major unrest. After President Mei Yiqi returned to Beiping the day before yesterday, he urged the professors to have a cordial conversation at Gongziying that night. The professors then dismissed the idea of resigning. As a result, the leaders of the petitioning students, namely Huang Cheng and other eleven members of the Student Union's National Salvation Committee, were each given two major demerits. President Mei Yiqi also convened a meeting of all students at 10:00 AM on the 24th to give a speech. After Mei's admonishment, the students were greatly moved. The details are summarized as follows.

Punishment of Students

The Tsinghua President's Office issued a notice stating: "On the afternoon of the 19th of this month, the Student Union's National Salvation Committee led many students to petition the Faculty Meeting, and then surrounded and coerced them, making a lot of noise and causing the entire faculty to resign. The order of our school has always been good, but these students have engaged in such undisciplined behavior, and it is directed at all teachers, which is a major mistake. The existence of a group depends on whether the members of the group abide by the discipline of the group, otherwise the group will collapse. Our school is one of the leading academic groups in the country, and the country and society have great expectations for our school. The President is responsible for maintaining order and enforcing discipline, and should enforce the law for such major acts of transgression. The members of the Student Union's National Salvation Committee, Huang Cheng, Chen Yuan, Liu Yuheng, Lu Cui, Gong Yuejian, Huang Riyi, Zhou Duoqi, Ye Dulian, Ding Zeliang, Wu Chengming, Liu Rujin, and others, should have been expelled immediately. Considering that these students have already deeply regretted their actions, they are each given two major demerits as a warning. From now on, we hope that you will be mindful of the difficult times and work together to overcome them, so that in these dark times, the teaching work of our school can still have the reality of its continuous effort, so as to extend the lifeline of the country and nation in academia. This is what all colleagues of our school should strive for together." This notice, President's Office.

Make-Up Exam Date

It is announced that the semester examination for the first semester of this academic year could not be held from February 24th according to the newly set school calendar due to the resignation of all professors. In addition to earnestly requesting the professors to return to their posts, the examination for the first semester has now been rescheduled to be held from February 29th to March 6th. Classes will be temporarily suspended from today until February 28th to allow for review of coursework. This notice, President Mei Yiqi. It is announced that the examination for the first semester of this academic year has now been rescheduled to be held on the 29th of this month. The next semester is scheduled to begin on March 9th. All newly ordered courses and special lectures will begin on the same day. This notice, President Mei Yiqi.

President's Speech

President Mei Yiqi's speech briefly stated that the student actions that occurred at the school were incorrect, and as the president, he must point them out to everyone, admonish everyone, and fulfill his due responsibilities. Colleagues and students in the school are all part of Tsinghua. Although they are in different positions, they are united in their love for Tsinghua. Tsinghua is what it is because of the efforts of past teachers and students. We should do our best to protect it and maintain it, but we must never let the indiscretion of current actions cause future harm. In a school, one should recognize the responsibilities of each other. Teachers use their own knowledge and skills to train everyone. Everyone comes to Tsinghua to study in order to obtain this kind of training. If you think that Tsinghua's training does not suit you, you do not have to reluctantly stay at Tsinghua. If you think that the school's training is not needed, you do not have to reluctantly stay either. School discipline is of utmost importance. In school, in order to make education truly meaningful, discipline must be maintained. Recently, students like to use the term "extraordinary times," as if everything can be done in an extraordinary way. However, they do not know that since we are now in extraordinary times, discipline is more important than usual. Everyone should also recognize this clearly. When the Faculty Meeting was held on the 19th, many students petitioned, surrounded and shouted, demanding exemption from examinations. Students should believe in, respect, and obey teachers. Coercion and insults are impolite. The teachers felt the most regret on that day was the destruction of the school's discipline, and they felt that it was impossible to continue teaching. I met with the professors last night, and I have expressed my apologies to everyone for the responsibilities I bear, but in order to maintain the school's discipline in the future, there must be a way to correct the students who were responsible on that day. Regarding the request for exemption from examinations, I can now state frankly to everyone that it is impossible. This matter has been considered repeatedly before. On the one hand, I considered the situation of the students, and on the other hand, I did not want to act hastily in the teaching career, so I postponed it again and again, but it is absolutely impossible not to take the exam. Now that the previously set exam date has been missed, we will have to wait another three to five days to ask the professors to return to their posts, and then we will hold it often. Regarding the issue of education in extraordinary times, I convened a discussion meeting with everyone on the 30th of last month, and I gave a general report on the principles set by the school, the hiring of many professors, the organization of a committee, and the situation of drafting a plan. The plan has now been drafted by the committee, and a detailed plan will be submitted to the Faculty Meeting for discussion before it can be implemented. The so-called education curriculum in extraordinary times only supplements the proper curriculum and does not replace the normal curriculum. In addition to the normal curriculum, I hope that you will study practical knowledge and skills. Recently, there have been many differences in opinion among the students. I hope that everyone can still cooperate, encourage each other, and strive to move towards rationality. At this time, my only responsibility is to seek the stability of the school and the normal progress of education. There are many difficulties at present, and we are now trying to gather all our strength to seek a solution.

Student Congress

President Mei Yiqi's speech ended at 11:00 AM. After Mei Yiqi, Pan Guangdan, and Shen Li left the meeting, Yang Liansheng, chairman of the school's student council, convened a general meeting of all students. The attendance was 810 people, and Yang Liansheng was elected as the chairman of the presidium, with Lu Cui as the presiding officer. A total of four proposals were raised: (1) to hold make-up exams in compliance with school regulations; (2) to implement the school's proposed education plan for extraordinary times; (3) to withdraw from the Student Union; and (4) to reconsider the case of female student Ji Yunxiu. However, all of them were rejected without discussion.
